# Publish Product Tables

This file contains documentation for 4 Databricks warehouse tables related to the Publish product functionality.
These tables track publishing events, workflows, and related data.

---

## narrative.core.publish

### Schema

| Column             | Type              | Nullable |
| ------------------ | ----------------- | -------- |
| Op                 | `StringType()`    | True     |
| id                 | `StringType()`    | True     |
| account_id         | `StringType()`    | True     |
| plan_id            | `StringType()`    | True     |
| name               | `StringType()`    | True     |
| stripe_sub_id      | `StringType()`    | True     |
| activation_date    | `TimestampType()` | True     |
| inserted_at        | `TimestampType()` | True     |
| updated_at         | `TimestampType()` | True     |
| interval           | `StringType()`    | True     |
| billing_status     | `StringType()`    | True     |
| stripe_status      | `StringType()`    | True     |
| has_used_trial     | `StringType()`    | True     |
| has_posted         | `StringType()`    | True     |
| legacy_account_id  | `StringType()`    | True     |
| legacy_migrated_at | `TimestampType()` | True     |
| \_rescued_data     | `StringType()`    | True     |

### Sample Row

```json
{
  "Op": "U",
  "id": "c7bc83a5-e20b-4dca-bad8-90b4eb16c310",
  "account_id": "7c1f9487-d089-4163-b4bc-63426e953fca",
  "plan_id": "f349b409-1959-44d4-a8f7-d707a326c1f0",
  "name": "Publish",
  "stripe_sub_id": "sub_1KlfjmGyxyMEWHozzgNWmspf",
  "activation_date": "NaT",
  "inserted_at": "2022-04-06 19:38:40",
  "updated_at": "2025-06-24 03:38:42",
  "interval": "year",
  "billing_status": "active",
  "stripe_status": "past_due",
  "has_used_trial": "false",
  "has_posted": "false",
  "legacy_account_id": null,
  "legacy_migrated_at": "NaT",
  "_rescued_data": null
}
```

---

## narrative.default.publish_events

### Schema

| Column                            | Type              | Nullable |
| --------------------------------- | ----------------- | -------- |
| id                                | `StringType()`    | True     |
| user_id                           | `StringType()`    | True     |
| account_id                        | `StringType()`    | True     |
| transaction_id                    | `StringType()`    | True     |
| topic                             | `StringType()`    | True     |
| data                              | `StringType()`    | True     |
| initialized_at                    | `TimestampType()` | True     |
| occurred_at                       | `TimestampType()` | True     |
| source                            | `StringType()`    | True     |
| inserted_at                       | `TimestampType()` | True     |
| updated_at                        | `TimestampType()` | True     |
| updated_date                      | `StringType()`    | True     |
| resource_id                       | `StringType()`    | True     |
| vsn                               | `IntegerType()`   | True     |
| meta_app_name                     | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_app_run_id                   | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_app_app_locale               | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_app_version_number           | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_app_version_channel          | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_app_version_number_array     | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_system_os                    | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_system_arch                  | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_system_machine_id            | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_system_os_version            | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_system_system_locale         | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_system_machine_timezone      | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_system_os_version_array      | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_location_region              | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_location_country             | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_location_continent           | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_app_install_id               | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_system_os_architecture       | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_system_os_build_number       | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_view_state_view_mode         | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_view_state_inspector_state   | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_view_state_project_zoom      | `FloatType()`     | True     |
| meta_settings_show_hidden_images  | `BooleanType()`   | True     |
| meta_settings_auto_add_new_images | `BooleanType()`   | True     |
| meta_settings_split_used_images   | `BooleanType()`   | True     |
| meta_plan_id                      | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_plan_name                    | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_plan_status                  | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_plan_feature_names           | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_product_id                   | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_product_name                 | `StringType()`    | True     |
| meta_product_status               | `StringType()`    | True     |
| \_rescued_data                    | `StringType()`    | True     |
